<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>
<s> half a woman of this and half of another world except when as now she is as irresponsible a bit of life as a little flowering weed growing out of a wall <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>

<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>
<s> half a woman of this and half of another world except when as now she is as irresponsible a bit of life as a little flowering weed growing out of a wall <\s>
<s> she stands looking at mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy with dancing eyes <\s>
<s> i've brought yer to morrer's trahsers <\s>
<s> y'nt yer finished wiv to dy's <\s>
<s> i want to tyke em <\s>
<s> drat this last one me old fengers <\s>
<s> i learnt some poytry to dy i did <\s>
<s> reciting with unction little lamb who myde thee <\s>
<s> dost thou know who myde thee gyve thee life and byde thee feed by the stream and oer the mead gyve the clothing of delight softest clothing woolly bright gyve thee such a tender voice myking all the vyles rejoice <\s>
<s> little lamb who myde thee <\s>
<s> dost thou know who myde thee <\s>
<s> tes wonderful what things they tache ya nowadays <\s>
<s> when i grow up i'm goin to ave a revolver an shoot the people that steals my jools <\s>
<s> deary me wherever du yu get yore notions <\s>
<s> an i'm goin to ride on as orse be'ind a man an i'm goin to ryce trynes in my motor car <\s>
<s> dryly ah yu'um gwine to be very busy that's sartin <\s>
<s> with a smile nao <\s>
<s> don they tache yu that there <\s>
<s> blending contempt and a lingering curiosity nao <\s>
<s> i can sing though <\s>
<s> let's ear yu then <\s>
<s> shaking her head i can ply the pianner <\s>
<s> i can ply a tune <\s>
<s> brahn's when she's gone aht <\s>
<s> well yu are gettin edjucation <\s>
<s> du they tache yu to love yore neighbours <\s>
<s> straying to the window mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy what's the moon <\s>
<s> us used to zay twas made o crame cheese <\s>
<s> might i have my note book <\s>
<s> lord william hands it back lord w <\s>
<s> and look here if there's anything when a fellow's fortunate and another's not he puts his hand into his breast pocket press <\s>
<s> but you see i shall have to write you up a bit lord william <\s>
<s> the old aristocracy you know what the public still expects if you were to lend me money you might feel lord w <\s>
<s> never should have dreamt press <\s>
<s> but it wouldn't do <\s>
<s> have you a photograph of yourself <\s>
<s> by the way has it occurred to you that there may be another bomb on the premises <\s>
<s> i'll have a look <\s>
<s> he looks at his watch and begins hurriedly searching the bins bending down and going on his knees <\s>
<s> the press reverses the notebook again and sketches him press <\s>
<s> lord william examines the foundations of his house <\s>
<s> a voice calls bill <\s>
<s> the press snaps the note book to and looks up <\s>
<s> there where the communication trench runs in stands a tall and elegant woman in the extreme of evening dress with presence of mind lady william <\s>
<s> you'll find lord william oh <\s>
<s> have you a photograph of him <\s>
<s> eyeing her er no i suppose not no <\s>
<s> he sidles past her and is gone lady w <\s>
<s> with lifted eyebrows bill <\s>
<s> emerging dusting his knees hallo nell <\s>
<s> i was just making sure there wasn't another bomb <\s>
<s> yes that's why i came dawn who was that person <\s>
<s> he looked awfully yellow <\s>
<s> i hope you haven't been giving yourself away <\s>
<s> dubiously well i don't know <\s>
<s> what did he ask you <\s>
<s> well what did you tell him <\s>
<s> that i'd been baptised but he promised not to put it down <\s>
<s> bill you are absurd <\s>
<s> she gives a light tittle laugh lord w <\s>
<s> i don't remember anything else except that it was quite natural we should be bombed don't you know <\s>
<s> why what harm have we done <\s>
<s> been born my dear <\s>
<s> suddenly serious i say nell how am i to tell what this fellow felt when he left that bomb here <\s>
<s> why do you want to <\s>
<s> out there one used to know what one's men felt <\s>
<s> staring my dear boy i really don't think you ought to see the press it always upsets you <\s>
<s> why should you and i be going to eat ourselves silly to improve the condition of the sweated when lady w <\s>
<s> calmly when they're going to improve ours if we don't look out <\s>
<s> we've got to get in first bill <\s>
<s> here we are and here we shall stay as if there'd never been a war <\s>
<s> well thank heaven there's no front to a revolution <\s>
<s> you and i can go to glory together this time <\s>
<s> anything that's on i'm to abate in <\s>
<s> no in rhyme too <\s>
<s> i say your dress <\s>
<s> yes poulder tried to stop me but i wasn't going to have you blown up without me <\s>
<s> you do look stunning <\s>
<s> give us a kiss <\s>
<s> starting back oh bill <\s>
<s> don't touch me your hands <\s>
<s> never mind my mouth's clean <\s>
<s> they stand about a yard apart and banding their faces towards each other kiss on the lips <\s>
<s> appearing suddenly from the communication trench and tip toeing silently between them oh mum <\s>
<s> you and daddy are wasting time <\s>
<s> dinner's ready you know <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>
<s> half a woman of this and half of another world except when as now she is as irresponsible a bit of life as a little flowering weed growing out of a wall <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>
<s> half a woman of this and half of another world except when as now she is as irresponsible a bit of life as a little flowering weed growing out of a wall <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>

<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>
<s> half a woman of this and half of another world except when as now she is as irresponsible a bit of life as a little flowering weed growing out of a wall <\s>
<s> she stands looking at mrs <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>

<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>
<s> half a woman of this and half of another world except when as now she is as irresponsible a bit of life as a little flowering weed growing out of a wall <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>

<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>
<s> she is eleven or twelve years old large eyed dark haired and sallow <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>
<s> a bed a cupboard a coloured portrait of queen victoria and of all things a fiddle hanging on the wall <\s>
<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>
<s> she sits with her back to the window through which in the last of the light the opposite side of the little grey street is visible under the evening sky where hangs one white cloud shaped like a horned beast <\s>
<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
<s> being old and lonely she has that habit of talking to herself distressing to those who cannot overhear <\s>
<s> from the smack of her tongue she was once a west country cottage woman from the look of her creased parchmenty face she was once a pretty girl with black eyes in which there is still much vitality <\s>
<s> the door is opened with difficulty and a little girl enters carrying a pile of unfinished corduroy trousers nearly as large as herself <\s>
<s> she puts them down against the wall and advances <\s>

<s> curtain act ii the single room of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in a small grey house in bethnal green the room of one cumbered by little save age and the crockery debris of the past <\s>

<s> by the side of old mrs <\s>
<s> lemmy in her chair is a pile of corduroy trousers her day's sweated sewing and a small table <\s>

<s> she is still sewing and her lips move <\s>
